 Today is the birth anniversary of Saadat Hasan Manto
 unka janm 11 may 1912 ko hua tha
 He was the largest Kalmanigar in Urdu
 unhone apni kalam se aisi rachanaaen likh daaleen jise aaj tak yaad kiya jaataa he

 aaie jaanate hai unke jivan se judi kuch khaas baaten
 
 
 - Manto was born in Ludhiana to a barrister family
 - 24 saal kii umr main urdu main unka choti kahaniyon kaa pehla sanskaran atishpaare chapa
 After the partition of India and Pakistan, he was accused of writing pornography in Pakistan, but was not proved guilty
 - pakistan ne unhen 'nishaan-e-imtiyaaj' se nawaja or unki yaad main dak tikat jari kiya

 phir 1931 main unhone hindu sabha college main daakhila liya
 Manto was just 7 years old when the Jallianwala Bagh massacre took place in 1919
 itani choti umr main bhi unke man main ye ghatana gahari chhap chhod gai thi
 Manto's evergreen creations revolutionized mind and hyper-sensitive heart made him Manto
 manto kii pehali kahani 'tamaasha' thi jo jaaliyanvaala baag kii ghatana se nikal kar ai thi
 The Jallianwala massacre seen from the eyes of a 7-year-old child was mentioned by Manto in 'tamasha'
 manto kii kahaniyantoba tech singh, khol do, ghate kaa sauda, halaal or jhatka, khabardaar, karaamaat, bekhabari kaa phayda, peshkash, communism, tamaasha, bu, thanda gosht, ghate kaa sauda, halaal or jhatka, khabardaar, karaamaat, bekhabari kaa phayda, peshkash, kaali salwar he
 His workspace was Manto's first original Urdu storybook published in 1936, titled 'atishapare'
 aligarh main manto adhik nahin thahar sake or ek saal puraa hone se pehle hi amritsar laut gayi

 unki likhi hui kahaniyaan ko puri tarah se samaj paanaa behad mushkil he
